 ' deshbhar menwastu va seva kar (gst)vyavastha lagu karne ke liye pehali baar vidheyak upie sarkaar ne 2011 main pesh kiya tha, jo ab bekaar ho gaya he
 The major differences between that old bill and the new bill passed in the colloquium on Wednesday are: 1
 2011 main pesh kiye gaye pehle vidheyak main ek sarvyaapee apratyaksh kar vyavastha se rajyon ko hone vaale nuksaan kii bharpai kaa praavdhaan nahin kiya gaya tha
 The current bill provides for compensation of five years for the states
 2
 The amended bill provides for an additional one percent tax for five years
 iskaa upyog us rajya ko atirikt muaavja dene ke liye hoga, jahaan kisi vastu kaa utpaadan hota he
 It was not provided in the original bill
 3
 Petroleum products and alcohol were excluded from the area of influence of the original bill, while the amended bill excludes petroleum products and alcohol as well as tobacco
 4
 The original bill had a one-third ratio for the quorum of the GST Council to be constituted under the chairmanship of the Finance Minister, this ratio has been increased to half of the members in the amended Bill
 5
 The amended bill regarding voting in the council meeting states that decisions can also be made with the support of one-fourth of the members, whereas the original bill had a consensus decision
 6
 The original bill provided for the constitution of a committee headed by a retired judge of the Supreme Court or the Chief Justice of a High Court to settle the dispute
 sanshodhit vidheyak main is praavdhaan ko hataa diya gaya he or vivaad nipataara kaa kaam parishad ke hawaale kar diya gaya he
 7
 mul vidheyak ko samvidhan ke 115wein sanshodhan ke rup main soochibaddh kiya gaya tha, jabaki sanshodhit vidheyak ko samvidhan ke 122wein sanshodhan ke rup main soochibaddh kiya gaya he
